Publishing World 124

Special Enlarged Edition of Architectural Monthly Sells Well - Since the publication of the special enlarged edition of the Architectural Monthly, Volume 1, Issue 3, various engineering agencies and university libraries in Shanghai and other places have been sending remittances to subscribe. Readers who have read it have also praised it in writing, praising it as a rare publication in the domestic architectural field. It is reported that the third issue has long been sold out, and the fourth issue will be published soon. Retail and subscription locations: Shanghai Architectural Society, Room 620, 6th Floor, Continental Emporium, Nanjing Road, Shanghai.

Infant Hygiene Quarterly - The Infant Hygiene Quarterly, published by the Yingrui Condensed Milk Company at No. 20 Suzhou Road, Shanghai, is compiled by experts and provides detailed guidance on infant rearing methods. It is reported that the thirteenth issue has now been published, with richer content than before and many new materials added, such as maxims on childcare, beautiful photographs of children, novels, cartoons, etc. The printing is exquisite, making it an artistic publication. It is given away free of charge, but there are few copies left. Those who wish to obtain a copy should send a letter to the company with a half-cent postage stamp for local addresses and a one-cent stamp for out-of-town addresses to cover postage costs.

Recent News from Guanghua Bookstore - New books published by Guanghua Bookstore on Fourth Road have always been appreciated by readers from all walks of life. It is learned that the bookstore has recently published a book entitled "Biography of Lenin," which describes the life of the world's great man Lenin and the process of his creation of Soviet Socialism. It was written by Trotsky, an important figure in the Russian Revolution, and the writing style is also humorous, so it is especially popular among young people. It is also reported that the bookstore's large gift event has been extended for two weeks. During the gift period, all purchases of books, whether published by this bookstore or others, that reach one yuan will receive a book coupon of one yuan and a stack of original manuscript paper. Therefore, business has been even more enthusiastic recently.

Free Subscription to Ningbo Min Guo Daily - The Ningbo Min Guo Daily newspaper, recognizing that many people from Ningbo reside in Shanghai and are concerned about their hometown, has established a distribution center in Shanghai to facilitate subscriptions for all sectors. The newspaper will be launched on April 1st, with a monthly price of one yuan and a yearly price of ten yuan. In addition, there will be a free trial reading day on the 25th of this month. Those who wish to read the newspaper on a trial basis should send a letter to Yang De at No. 43 Tongfeng Lane, Dapu Bridge. Those who subscribe for the entire year before April 1st will receive one hundred cards and will have their names printed on them as a memento. In addition, a few salespersons are being recruited, with generous commissions but no lodging, board, or salary. Those who are interested should apply by mail to the above address.

Saturday Newspaper Donation Fee Deadline Tomorrow 125

The donation fee for one month of the Saturday newspaper at No. 311 Shandong Road to benefit aviation and national salvation will expire tomorrow and will be closed immediately. Starting next week, it will be handled as usual. Direct subscriptions to the newspaper for the entire year (52 issues) cost one yuan domestically and three yuan and five jiao overseas. Issues 44 and 45 are published today, with illustrated materials and paper that are printed with extreme care, comparable to European and American publications. All newspaper vendors are selling the publication.

Fire on Zhoujiazui Road 126

Last night at around 7 p.m., a fire broke out accidentally at a certain lumberyard located at Nos. 101 to 102 Zhoujiazui Road, Yangshupu. Smoke and fog spread quickly, and flames shot out in all directions. Two houses were destroyed, but the fire was extinguished after firefighters rushed to the scene.

Reuters, London, 17th - Today, the price of silver here has decreased. Recent silver is at 17 pence 625, and forward silver is at 17 pence 6875. Both recent and forward silver have decreased by 25 from yesterday.

London to New York exchange rates at 3 p.m. today were as follows: one British pound equals 3.4625 U.S. dollars, and one U.S. dollar equals 5 shillings and 9.314 pence.

New York, 17th - The opening price for forward silver in the market here today decreased by 10 to 80 pounds from yesterday's closing price.

Weather Report 128

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 p.m. yesterday stated: The weather on the Shandong coast is uncertain, with strong cyclones, rain, or yellow sand. In the middle and lower reaches of the Yangtze River, the sky is cloudy and mild, with tight southeasterly to southwesterly winds. Along the coast south of Ma'anshan Island, the sky is cloudy and the wind is gentle and directionless. Also, the local temperature for the 24 hours before 2 p.m. yesterday was 49.9 degrees at its highest and 32.4 at its lowest. On the same day last year, the high was 58.3 and the low was 36.3.

Reader Advisor

Two Triangular Love Problems 129

Mr. He Chao-min and Mr. Yan's Correspondence

To put it briefly: There is a male, A, and a female, B, who have been together for two years, and both families have tacitly acknowledged the possibility of marriage. Recently, female B has fallen in love with male C and disregarded male A. The reason for her change of heart is, of course, that she feels the past was a mistake, that she was blind. Theoretically speaking: once male A knows this, it's best to (give up). Because this kind of thing simply cannot be forced. Unexpectedly, male A has poor judgment and is extremely possessive. Female B, fearing slander because her relationship with male A is already known among family and friends, reluctantly agrees to male A's wish and gets formally engaged. However, she is in great pain in her heart and still cannot forget male C. Male C, on the other hand, is a man who has been through countless hardships, suffering all kinds of experiences and is almost thirty years old. He naturally accepts her passion. However, he doesn't want to embarrass male A. Therefore, he not only doesn't encourage her to move forward but instead tries to help male A and female B restore their old relationship. At the same time, he tells female B, "Let's treat each other as brother and sister from now on, and don't think of anything else." However, female B seems dissatisfied with this implicitly. Sir, in this situation, which path should female B take? Which path should male C take?

Answer: In the reporter's opinion, the happiness of a love triangle probably cannot compensate for the degree of pain, and I very much hope you won't meddle in this kind of trivial matter. Aren't you hearing daily at the telegraph office the alarming news of the fall of Rehe, the loss of Chengde, the imminent danger of Beiping and Tianjin, and the destruction of the country? How can you still have the interest to discuss this kind of problem? As we see it, whether Zhang San is good with her or not; whether Li Si is good with her or not; whether male A is good with female B or not; whether male C is good with female B or not; whether both male A and male C are good with her or not, as long as they have no complaints against each other and each gets what they want, any path is fine. What else is there to discuss? This time, with the fall of Rehe, some people in the Shanghai newspapers blamed Zhang Xueliang, saying he was "(indulging in singing, dancing, and entertainment)". However, without unenterprising citizens who don't sing, dance, and entertain, how could there be such high-ranking officials who indulge in singing, dancing, and entertainment? I hope you will think deeply and wake up!

When I first came to Shanghai, I was introduced to a few female compatriots by friends. Among them were two sisters surnamed Zhu. The elder Zhu and I were classmates and even had the same elective courses, so we had many opportunities to get close. After a semester, we had developed a very good relationship. Once, when it was just the two of us playing in the room, she suddenly brought up some questions about love to discuss with me. At the same time, she frankly expressed her theories about love that she had never talked about with me before. At the time, I didn't feel anything special. Later, I slowly realized that she was very interested, and based on her recent attitude and actions, I could determine that she was signaling to me, challenging me. Driven by curiosity, I subtly revealed a kind of resistant attitude to her. She was already fully prepared, waiting with her bow drawn to the full, and sure enough, it was triggered with a single touch. After that, our friendship gained a component of love. After about another semester, although our love had reached a considerable degree, I always felt somewhat dissatisfied with her: first, she was too quiet, completely lacking a naive and innocent attitude; second, she was two years older than me (according to the physiological age for male and female marriage, the female should be younger than the male). At first, I didn't feel anything, but later I felt distressed everywhere and didn't get any enjoyment from the relationship. If I wanted to reject her, she was always very good to me, and I couldn't bear to reject her because of my feelings. Because our residences were very close, I often met her younger sister when she came to visit her. She (the younger Zhu) was a naive and lively virgin who had just come of age. She was certainly prettier than the elder Zhu, and also very healthy, but her knowledge and experience were not as good as her sister's. At first, I had some ambitions towards her, but because I had developed that kind of relationship with the elder Zhu, I gave up on this idea. However, when I felt that I couldn't continue with the elder Zhu, my old thoughts arose again, and I decided to change my strategy and attack the younger Zhu. Things went very smoothly. As soon as I signaled to her, she indicated her acceptance. However, she already knew about my relationship with the elder Zhu, and at first, she suspected that I wasn't serious. After I explained it to her repeatedly, she believed me. In this way, the younger Zhu and I went from friends to love again. After that, I subtly showed coldness towards the elder Zhu. She was baffled. Then I told her about my relationship with the younger Zhu. She was extremely angry and cried for two days. But she still didn't want to break up with me and instead blamed me for being unfaithful. Later, she often insulted and scolded the younger Zhu and declared that if I married the younger Zhu, she would definitely ask her parents to cut off the younger Zhu's financial support (because their parents loved the elder Zhu more, so she could say this and do it). As I see it: although I am somewhat dissatisfied with the elder Zhu, she is indeed more considerate at times. However, it should be easier to reject her, because our relationship was initiated by her challenging me and me resisting. But I couldn't bear to reject her because of my feelings. On the younger Zhu's side, I was the one who issued the challenge, and I was the one who launched the attack. Since she has accepted my love, of course, I can't let her down, so I might as well marry her. But what if her financial support is really cut off? My finances can't support the needs of two people. So I am really in a dilemma. They are also feeling great pain, and the sisters' relationship is deteriorating day by day. I don't know what to do. Now I propose a few points, and please, sir, be sure to teach me what to do: 1. Should I break off with both of them? Or should I make one of them happy? 2. If I adopt the latter question, which one should I make happy? 3. After making one happy, how should I deal with the other? 4. After making one happy, if the other unfortunately stages a tragedy, what legal responsibility should I bear? 5. Is it reasonable to reject both of them? After rejecting them, how should I handle myself? How should I deal with them?

Answer: Since you developed a relationship with the elder Zhu, you shouldn't have gone on to attack the younger Zhu. Now you have one foot on two boats. Is this a matter for Qi or Chu? It's no wonder it's difficult for you to please everyone. An outsider cannot answer this kind of question for you. It is best to solve it yourself. However, since you have asked, we have no choice but to briefly offer our views as follows: 1. It is best to reject both of them and turn back to focus on your studies. A young man who is trapped in a love net will ruin his life. 2. If you can't reject them both, you must decide who to welcome and who to reject between the two: If you are thinking of yourself, you should still abandon the younger Zhu and take the elder Zhu. Because the elder Zhu was the one who attacked you, and she is two years older than you. She naturally knows this shortcoming. Therefore, her feelings for you must be more sincere and more reliable. Her quietness and taciturnity are not her shortcomings, but her strengths. It is good to be naive and innocent, but precisely because she is naive and innocent, she is also easily swayed. (You can't have both). Give up the fish and take the bear's paw.) Do you think so?

Education News

Important News 130

The Shandong Education Circle Establishes an Anti-Japanese

Troop慰労Association

Donations and Purchases are Sent to the Front Lines

(Jinan, 17th) The Education Department initiated the Shandong Education Circle Anti-Japanese Troop慰労Association. The inaugural meeting was held at the Education Department at 9 a.m. today. The secretary-general of the Education Department, Wang Ziyu, presided over the meeting. Wang Zhengxuan and six others were appointed as standing committee members. Regulations were established for one-time donations: those with monthly salaries below 30 yuan would donate 6 jiao; those with salaries between 31 and 50 yuan would donate 1 yuan; those with salaries between 51 and 100 yuan would donate 6%; those with salaries between 101 and 200 yuan would donate 12%; those with salaries between 201 and 300 yuan would donate 16%; those with salaries between 301 and 400 yuan would donate 20%; and those with salaries above 401 yuan would donate 24%. Notices have been sent to all secondary schools and county education bureaus inside and outside the province to comply. Education Department and county/city education bureau staff who have already paid six months of machine donations will donate an additional month this month, based on the amount of the airplane donation. The Education Department has already started donating funds today, totaling 5,731.30 yuan. In the future, the total amount of donations will be used to purchase food produced in the province and send personnel to the front-line military hospitals.

Sun Yat-sen and Tongji Universities

Form Medical Teams to Go North 131

(Nanjing, 17th) Guangzhou's Sun Yat-sen University replied to Dai Chuanxian and Zhu Jiahua, immediately organizing a medical team to go north to work in the war zone. Dai and Zhu also plan to establish a rear hospital for Sun Yat-sen University at a suitable location, with the entire medical team serving in the hospital. In addition, the medical team organized by Tongji University has been established, with 12 faculty members and 112 students participating. After the Sun Yat-sen University medical team arrives in the north, they will jointly proceed to the front lines.

Foreign Teachers Not Deducted Airplane Donation 132

(Nanjing, 17th) The Ministry of Education, based on the National Music Academy's inquiry about whether foreign teachers, who make up more than half of the faculty, should be deducted for the national salvation airplane donation, submitted a request to the Executive Yuan. The directive stated that foreign teachers should not be deducted for the national salvation airplane donation. Orders have been issued to all national universities and colleges to comply.

Guo Renyuan Addresses Teachers and Students

Guo Renyuan, the newly appointed president of National Zhejiang University, went to the university yesterday to take over and assume his duties. At 11 a.m., he convened all faculty, staff, and students from the College of Engineering and the College of Arts and Sciences in the auditorium to give a speech, with many words of encouragement. Ministry Inspectors Inspect Anhui Education Situation 134

Ministry of Education inspectors Tang Xifen and others came to Anhui on the 8th to conduct inspections. Yesterday, they completed the inspection of various educational institutions in the provincial capital. On the afternoon of the 12th, they convened the principals of various schools in the provincial capital to report their inspection opinions. Tang's criticisms of education in the province were generally as follows: Strengths: (1. Teachers are mostly full-time and less part-time, with not too short tenures; 2. Staff are generally able to work on time; 3. Students generally maintain order in class and during self-study, especially students at No. 1 Middle School.) Weaknesses: (1. Too few charts and instruments; 2. Improper allocation of funds; 3. Too much rote learning; 4. Insufficient student labor; 5. Inconsistent teaching and discipline.) After the criticisms, he reported the Ministry of Education's recent methods for reforming schools at all levels.

Minutes of the Municipal Boy Scout Council Meeting 135

Followed by a Series of Group Leader Meetings

The Municipal Boy Scout Council held its 20th council meeting yesterday afternoon at the Moore Memorial Church on Tibet Road. Council members Tong Xingbai, Qu Yue, Leng Xueqiao, Zhang Xunfang, Wang Zhao Wei-zu attended. Leng Xueqiao chaired and Xie Yanbo recorded. Formalities were observed. A. Report Items: 1. Condolences for the four Boy Scouts who died in the Shanghai Incident; the Garrison Committee's letter reported the conclusion; 2. The General Association's office has approved the establishment of a design committee; 3. The General Association's preparatory office has ordered the re-election and instructed the submission of a service member roster; 4. The Municipal Education Bureau's reply regarding the allocation of a camp site in the central area of the city has been forwarded to the municipal government; 5. The General Association's preparatory office has ordered the collection and mailing of catalogs of Boy Scout publications and supplies; 6. Headquarters instruction: Commander Chiang Kai-shek's inauguration and use of the seal; 7. The General Association's preparatory office instructed to organize war zone service groups; various regulations are being drafted and await orders to be followed; 8. The General Association's preparatory office informed that there is no need to discuss increasing the number of council members; 9. The General Association's preparatory office informed to extend the term of council members, to be considered for adoption; 10. Status of service members reporting for duty. B. Discussion Items: 1. Wu Gang and others petitioned to restore the war zone service group, to go north to serve immediately. Resolved: Reply based on the instructions from the General Association's preparatory office; 2. Zhejiang Province's Second Grand Review and Camporee seeks prizes. Resolved: Assigned to standing committee members to handle; 3. The preparatory committee for the condolence meeting for the four Boy Scouts who died in the Shanghai Incident reported the conclusion of the event, requesting investigation and handling. Resolved: Forwarded to the General Association's preparatory office for review and handling; 4. Request to confirm the list of members of the council's design committee and to recommend members to draft organizational conditions. Resolved: Assigned to standing committee members to nominate and determine regulations for submission at the next meeting; 5. Request to submit to the General Association's preparatory office to promptly promulgate the organizational regulations and training methods for the war zone affairs groups. Resolved: Approved; 6. The council's fundraising committee for the China Boy Scout Airplane Fund proposed to actively carry out fundraising work, now recommending council member Tong Xingbai to contact the Aviation Association to discuss implementation methods, and separately recommending council members Leng Xueqiao and Luo Lie to draft fundraising methods for approval. Resolved: Approved. After the discussion, the city-wide group leader meeting was immediately held to report on the progress of various Boy Scout activities, methods to assist the Aviation Association in publicity, and finally to discuss the organization and training methods for war zone service, to be submitted to the council for adoption.

Yesterday at Southeast Women's Physical Education Teachers College, Liangjiang Women's Physical Education Teachers College, and Dongya Physical Education College. Boy Scout expert Zhang Zhongren, former commander of the Chinese Kuomintang Boy Scouts, has been lecturing and hosting receptions at the request of various schools, societies, and Boy Scout circles in the city since arriving in Shanghai last week. Yesterday morning, Mr. Zhang gave a lecture at the invitation of the 121st Regiment of the Chinese Boy Scouts of the Southeast Women's Physical Education Teachers College. The entire school attended the lecture, which lasted for two hours. In the afternoon, he agreed to the invitation of the 196th Regiment of the Chinese Boy Scouts of the Liangjiang Women's Physical Education Teachers College and the 250th Regiment of Dongya Physical Education College to lecture at the two regiments. Mr. Zhang's arguments were thorough and his views were innovative. He gave a very fair exposition on the current Boy Scout cause, which was highly admired by the students. It is reported that Mr. Zhang will visit Shanghai Middle School of Jiangsu Province tomorrow to give a lecture.

Actively Fundraising for the 137

Shanghai School No. 1 Airplane

Schools Implement Monthly Donations in Accordance with the Methods

The Shanghai Education Association initiated the fundraising for the Shanghai School No. 1 Airplane. Since establishing the methods and distributing them to major and minor schools throughout the city, and since starting fundraising separately from March 1st, the schools have all implemented monthly donations for teachers, staff, and students in accordance with the methods. The first phase of the donation is scheduled to end on May 31st, and it is estimated that 80,000 yuan can be raised. The second phase will be fundraised from August 1st to the end of November. It is expected that one airplane can be completed within the year.

The Municipal Education Bureau 138

Establishes a Public Radio Listening Post

Address: Community Education Center

The Municipal Education Bureau, in order to promote continuing education, has established a radio broadcasting tutorial class. Its purpose is to enable people scattered in all directions to freely listen to lectures on the radio, thereby helping them to supplement their knowledge and skills in their spare time. At the beginning of the program, quite a few people signed up to learn. Now it is learned that ordinary commercial firms and factories, due to financial constraints, cannot purchase radio receivers for the time being, so that ordinary employees and apprentices, even if they are interested in learning, have no means to receive education, and many sigh with frustration. There are many people who are unable to do so. Therefore, a radio receiver has been installed in the lecture hall of the Community Education Center in Wenmiao, South Shanghai, as a public radio listening post. The scope of radio reception is limited to the three programs (Citizenship), (National Language), and (English) broadcast by the bureau's radio broadcasting tutorial class. Every evening from 9 p.m. to 10 p.m. is the public listening time. All students who have registered for the bureau's radio tutorial class can present their learning certificate and go to listen on time.

University Faculty and Staff Associations 140

General Membership Meeting to be Held Tomorrow

The Shanghai University Faculty and Staff Associations will hold a general membership meeting tomorrow (the 19th), as reported in yesterday's newspaper. The following is a summary of the association's founding process, which is published for the reference of people from all walks of life: 1. At 3:30 p.m. on December 16, 1931, a meeting of initiators was held at the YMCA in Ba Xian Qiao. More than 70 people from 16 universities attended. Chu Minyi chaired the meeting. Hu Shuhua, Zhang Shouyong, Jiang Zhensan, Lin Zhongke, Zheng Hongnian, Sheng Zhenwei, Kang Xuanyi, Wang Zaoshi, Chu Minyi, and He Tingshu were elected as members of the preparatory committee. 2. At 12 noon on February 18th, the first meeting of the preparatory committee was held at the Hua'an Building. Hu Shuhua chaired the meeting, allocated duties, and appointed Kang Yi and He Tingshu as members of the declaration and charter drafting committee. 3. At 4:30 p.m. on February 23rd, the second preparatory committee meeting was held at the Hua'an Building. Zheng Hongnian chaired the meeting. Kang Xuanyi explained the drafting process, the draft charter was passed, and the date of establishment was determined. 4. At 10 a.m. on February 28th, an establishment meeting was held at the YMCA. More than 300 members from various schools attended. Chu Minyi chaired the meeting, the charter was passed, and Chu Minyi, Wang Jingqi, Zheng Hongnian, Hu Shuhua, Kang Xuanyi, Li Yingji, Zhang Shouyong, Lin Tongying, Li Denghui, Lin Zhongke, Fan Shouchi, Jiang Zhensan, Chen Qifu, Tang Ying, He Tingshu, Wu Qishan, Sun Boqian, Wang Yao, Zhang Yuanruo, Yuan Zhu, Bo Chenqun, Yan Fuqing, Zhang Wenfu, Yang Yufen, Han Yanmen, Hu Yaomei, Chen Xiangzun, Huang Xianzhang, Zheng Zhongying, etc. were elected as members. Representatives. A number of Wu Zijing, Yang Bangdong, He Shimo, Ma Shouzheng, Ma Shouchun, He Shizhen, Yu Rixuan, Yu Senwen, Zhou Changxian, Lu Jizeng, etc. By the end of the year, representatives of teachers and staff who reported to the various schools included Ma Shouzheng and Chen Genlu of Labor University, Chen Zhongfan and Ye Yuan of Jinan University, Lu Xiyan and He Liang of Tongji University, Wang Zaoshi and Rong Qizhao of Guanghua University, Fan Zhongyun of Zhonggong University, Dai Yunwen of the Business School of China University, Li Peifu of the Cultural Academy, Liu Hairuo of the Shanghai Art College, Zhu Futing of the Political Science College, Li Zuwei of the Southeast Medical College, Bao Xueliang of the Shanghai Art College, Nong Ruxian of the Sino-French Institute of Technology, and specialists of the Sino-French Medical College. 5. At 4 p.m. on January 8, 1932, the third preparatory committee meeting was held at the YMCA. Hu Shuhua chaired the meeting and resolved to postpone the representative conference and appoint Kang Xuanyi to represent the association at the university presidents' dinner. 6. At 4 p.m. on January 19th, the fourth preparatory committee meeting was held at the YMCA. Due to insufficient attendance, it was changed to a discussion meeting. Zhang Shouyong chaired the meeting and decided to send letters urging various schools to produce representatives. 7. At 4 p.m. on January 24th, the fifth preparatory committee meeting was held at the Sino-French Institute of Technology. It was decided to hold the representative conference at the YMCA on February 14th. Later, due to representatives being scattered during the war and financial difficulties at various schools, it was impossible to convene. 8. At 11 a.m. on March 12, 1933, the sixth preparatory committee meeting was held at the YMCA. It was decided to hold the first general membership meeting at noon on the 19th of this month.

Shanghai Girls' Middle School National Salvation Donation 141

Decision to Submit to the Municipal Education Bureau for Distribution

All teachers and students of Shanghai Girls' Middle School on Xieqiao Manufacturing Bureau Road in the Nanshi district are very enthusiastic about the national salvation movement. Since the September 18th Incident two years ago, a large sum of money has been raised to donate to General Ma Zhanshan. Later, because General Ma withdrew to Russia, there was a balance of 514.89 yuan, which was kept in the Shanghai Bank by Chairman Lin Kanghou, a school director. Last year, 460.042 yuan was donated by the daily savings and frugality accounting, totaling 560.932 yuan. Now, the student union executive committee has decided to discuss with Chairman Lin Kanghou, the school director, to hand over all of the funds to the Education Bureau for distribution and donation to the national salvation cause.

Jointly Written by More Than Thirty Famous Educators Nationwide 143

Revised (Student Guide) Published

Cai Yuanpei Praises It, Saying (Cherishing Students with Virtue to Perfect Their Excellence)

The (Student Guide), edited by the Shanghai Qinfen Bookstore with the invitation of national education experts, has long been popular throughout the country since its publication and has been well received by college and middle school students nationwide. It is now heard that a revised edition has been published, with greatly enriched content. Zhou Fohai, Tai Shuangqiu, Hu Shuhua, Yu Jitai, and others have been additionally invited to contribute articles such as the Student Guide for Educational Colleges, the Student Guide for Ding Colleges, and the Student Guide for Science Colleges, which are quite valuable. The guide is divided into upper and lower volumes. Spring and Autumn

Only Hear the Escalator Sounding 160

— Xianxian

No One Seen Coming Down

"Only hear the escalator sounding, no one seen coming down," these are two local sayings of us Suzhou people, also symbolizing the emptiness of us Suzhou people. Unexpectedly, these two sentences, by this time, have a great effect of changing customs, empty-headedness, prevailing globally, empty-headedness, lasting for thousands of years.

After September 18th, China and Japan dragged and pulled each other to Geneva. At that time, that old League of Nations gentleman, with his beard standing on end, slammed the gavel with a thunderous sound, saying that the violent Japan must be sanctioned. From then on, until now, the Japanese demonstrate once to the old League of Nations gentleman, and the old League of Nations gentleman also demonstrates once. But the old League of Nations gentleman, despite repeatedly rising in anger, still sits motionless. The escalator keeps sounding, but people still don't come down.

On January 28th, the 19th Route Army and the 5th Army resisted Japan. The Japanese army dispatched the 横一師團 and 竪一師團 divisions, and the Chinese people looked forward to the arrival of reinforcements from all sides day and night, to resist the strong enemy. So when it was heard that a certain army had arrived in Suzhou, and a certain army had arrived in Wuxi, although defending outside the 30th and 40th defense lines, everyone was excited and danced with joy. Who knew that such news kept coming, and until the Chinese army retreated to 20 miles away, the troops standing on the front line and in the rear never saw a face from another army. The escalator sounded really solid, consistent from beginning to end, but no reinforcements came.

National crisis, national crisis, has now been a year and a half, spending days and nights enduring hardships, recovering lost territory, but now the national crisis remains like a vast land. Whether the established policy is long or short-term, has never been revealed. The sound of the escalator is like someone is coming down, but unfortunately, no one has come down in the end.

"Only hear the escalator sounding, no one seen coming down," may become a kind of cosmopolitanism in the future, and my Suzhou emptiness has glory in it.

The Poison of Words 161

— Chi Fo

To live one's life based on the position of books, thinking oneself to be perfectly reasonable, will inevitably lead to a dead end. This is something I have learned from experience, and perhaps modern youth feel the same pain. Originally, learning is learning, experience is experience, the best students in school are not necessarily the great men of society in the future; the great men in society, even though they are inferior students in school; the saying that education does not create talents, I cannot accept.

Words are originally a sharp weapon for killing genius. At the same time, people who know how to read and understand reason are also an obstacle in the philosophy of life. If we don't read, know how to read, and understand reason, living muddleheaded, eating when hungry, and shitting when full, only knowing how to make money and get rich, regardless of cruel means and despicable behavior; flattering, bragging, crawling through dog holes, wagging our tails and begging for mercy, flattering and smiling obsequiously, only seeking to achieve the purpose of making money and getting rich, how can we care about the filthiness of the means? This is not necessarily scolding them for being shameless, in fact, their brains only contain the four words (make money and get rich), so their behavior is like this.

Friends who read books have many theories deeply engraved in their minds, such as Mozi's doctrine of universal love, Laozi's doctrine of non-action, the Buddhist view of emptiness in all things, as well as the Jin people's wild and reckless behavior, the Song Confucian's rectification of the heart and sincerity of intention, Tao Yuanliang, Bai Juyi, Shao Yaofu, Lu Fangweng's reclusion, Sima Xiangru, Cao Zijian, Yuan Wei, Hou Chaozong, Mao Pijiang's unrestrainedness; putting many theories into a small brain, thinking that one has mastered ancient and modern knowledge and is full of learning, how can one know that in the eyes of modern fashionable friends, is it not a person who has gone insane?

Therefore, in order to enable our children and grandchildren to stand firm in modern society in the future, to have food to eat, clothes to wear, become great men, and make a fortune, never let them read books, never let them know how to read. Understanding the principles of the book temple will make one ignorant of the principles of eating and making a fortune. After all, a person is born into the world, eating is important, making a fortune is important, never be poisoned by (the poison of words), this is a sentence of experience from me, I respectfully advise you all to remember!

Rose Thorn 162

— Zui Zhu

(The territory of Rehe is lovely, the old soil of Rehe is even more lovely. If you can't have both, what should I take? Take the old soil!)

So Tang Yulin passed away!

The pocket money of elementary school students, the flower money of little girls, the sweat and blood money of ordinary people, the hard-earned money of small employees, are all being thought of by someone.

The sinful money of the big masters, the heavy interest money of the big landlords, the unconscionable money of the big rich men, the black-hearted money of the big bureaucrats, the big local tyrants (opium soil tyrants), no one dares to touch a hair on them.

This is called (the death of the big old and small is equal to the fresh and alive dead man, the ignorant little ones, just come to make trouble and stir up the energy.)

Other people's planes are busy in the sky,

Our planes are flexing their muscles in the newspapers,

Buddha! Just get a plane for us to see, so we know where the money went!

Full-Length Novel

Fourth Company Commander of the Northeast 163

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Two

A humble room makes for fragrant neighbors, secretly admiring the healthy old man. The Quan family chooses a good match, vehemently criticizing the poor child.

Guizhi smiled and said: "That's not necessarily true, I've heard of girls who don't leave home until they're a hundred years old!" It's really a coincidence in the world, just as Guizhi was saying a few words, Brother Ku Er across the street happened to come. Guizhi expected that the last sentence would definitely be heard by someone, and for some reason, her face turned red for a while. It was Brother Gan Er who spoke first, saying: "It's getting lively here, another neighbor has moved in." Guizhi said: "There are very few people in Company Commander Zhao's family, just his old man and a servant. Company Commander Zhao himself doesn't come home." Brother Gan Er smiled and said: "How can a soldier live at home? However, it's very close to his camp from here, and he can come home every day during the day, which is fine," as he looked Guizhi up and down. Although his words seemed very ordinary, the tone of his voice was inevitably barbed. Without saying anything, he gave her a slight glance, and then said: "Brother Er, are you here to pick up your clothes? They're not ready yet, they'll be done tomorrow." Brother Gan Er agreed with a "okay" and immediately went back. Jiang didn't care, and went about her business. Only Guizhi felt a little uncomfortable in her heart, feeling that moving in such a neighbor in the same courtyard inevitably offended a neighbor across the street. So, in her heart, she warned herself that she should go to the Zhao family's courtyard less often in the future, so as not to cause any trouble. Therefore, Guizhi only worked on the kang that afternoon and didn't go out. However, the Zhao family's servant kept coming, asking where to buy coal and where to call for water, coming a total of more than ten times. In the evening, the servant brought a large plate of hot steamed buns, saying that they were for Old Lady Yang. Jiang said to Guizhi: "This must be that old man feeling that he troubled us too much today, so he sent some things to return our favor, the old man is really polite." Guizhi said: "We thought that people who are military officers must be unreasonable, but judging from this, they're not bad." Jiang said: "That's right, I have to go see them tomorrow morning." Guizhi said: "Our neighbors are all pretty good, look, isn't the Gan family across the street very good too?" Jiang wanted to say something to her, saying that no matter what you say, you can't forget the Gan family, but then she thought that if she said this, the girl would be unhappy, so she held back and didn't say anything more. (15)

Obituary 164

— Zhao Ziming

The usual beginning of an obituary says: (The unfilial, burdened with sin, could not bring themselves to perish┋┋). However, when parents are alive, they are often made to feel hurt, angry, and to suffer. Once they pass away, it is grandly written (Burdened with sin, could not bring themselves to perish, disaster extends┋┋) to inform distant relatives and friends, in an attempt to absolve oneself of guilt. However, given the reality, can one really deceive others just by admitting to the weight of their sins? Then it goes on to say: (The deceased was bestowed the title of First Rank Official┋┋). The Qing Emperor has long since vanished. Why still refer to someone as a First Rank or Second Rank Lady┋┋? Even if one achieved the title of Special Rank Lady, what glory is there in that?

It also says: (The unfilial ones are employed at the Provincial Government, studied abroad, and upon hearing the news, rushed back by electric dispatch that very night). This is merely to show that your two young masters are high officials and foreign PhDs. That your sons could rush back that very night is considered filial piety, enough to make you smile in your grave. But whether the night had shining stars or torrential rain is unknown to outsiders. However, with convenient transportation today, with trains and airplanes going back and forth, even rushing back on a snowy night is not painful!

The end is still laden with lonely orphans, mourning sons, heavy mourning, light mourning, shedding blood, bowing reverently, wiping tears and kowtowing┋┋. If everyone truly squeezed out bright red blood from their eyes, that would be terrifying. If parents have kind hearts, even in eternal sleep, they would not wish their children and grandchildren to do such a thing!

Some can't wait for their parents to die so they can divide the inheritance. At that time, they won't shed blood, they won't even shed a single tear! In the end, is it about saving face or striving for glory while alive? In short, obituaries should eliminate falsehood and adopt a new style. They can also represent whether society is progressing, so they are worth promoting and improving!

Miscellaneous Talk

Nine-Flavor Tea 165

— Zhang Yian

Students always feel that teachers are somewhat mysterious. Is this a religious effect?

Law is recognized by society as the most powerful thing. As long as it is legal, there is nothing wrong with it. However, judging from the matter of marriage, it seems to require many conditions beyond the law.

At wedding banquets or when teasing the newlyweds, the most enthusiastic and excited ones are always unmarried young men! Admiration, jealousy, and curiosity condense into a thick and intense feeling at this time. As for married people, they mostly express indifference in such situations. Women, as a rule, are unwilling to express anything.

Young people often have abundant energy, while older people often lack it. Those with abundant energy naturally have a strong urge to vent it, and they do so to the fullest when they have the opportunity. Rushing about, laughing, and joking are all expressions of young people venting their excess energy. Those with insufficient energy remain still and inactive, even feeling disgusted when they see others active, and if it is within their power, they may even forbid or prevent it. Therefore, people who are too far apart in age and do not understand each other cannot get along.

In Japan, the way Japanese people pass the time when riding the train is by reading newspapers and magazines. In Shanghai's trams, although there are also a few people reading newspapers, there are very few. They seem to each have their own boredom, each have their own feelings. The only pastime for male passengers is to stare at young and beautiful female passengers.

Time can cause people to develop feelings and relationships. Because the time spent on the tram is often so short, it is not easy for passengers to develop good feelings or relationships with each other. Sometimes they may exchange a few words, but they are all insignificant or even contain suspicion. The situation is closer and it is easier for people to develop a sense of community on long-distance trains or ships.

In the area of the Shanghai-Hangzhou and Beijing-Shanghai railways, you can see many pines and cypresses and tombs. These pines and cypresses and tombs seem to depend on each other for survival. It is not known whether earthen tombs were built because there were pines and cypresses, or whether pines and cypresses were planted because there were tombs. The tombs seen in Guangdong are bare and without a single tree, and even weeds are removed. (The tomb trees are already large). This saying is probably not something that can be experienced in Guangdong. Photography is a chance coincidence of time and space.

When urinating, young students are very eager to see the secrets of older classmates.

A skilled vendor in a movie theater. He can recognize which viewers need to buy his things. He can squeeze in and out of rows of seats filled with customers without causing intolerable annoyance from the seated customers. He can reach out a long distance to take the money given by the customer, and at the same time give the customer the goods they need. He can distinguish the good from the bad of coins and banknotes in a very cramped space. He can say a few English words, although not grammatically correct, that can express what his industry requires. He can pay attention to adults with children, as they are mostly good customers. He can use his keen hearing to respond to the soft call of a customer sitting far away.

The way to write the character (車) is different from the character (車). It was created by Cantonese people. The character (車) is read in the ancient tone as (居), while the character (車) is read in the modern way of saying the car, like (奢) (in Guangzhou, the car is pronounced the same as the luxury character). Although the meaning is absolutely the same, it is not bad to be able to distinguish it in pronunciation.

The (grand signature) on the guest book is the most skilled and energetic calligraphy that everyone writes, and everyone will think that my (grand signature) will definitely arouse the appreciation of others. This psychology is expressed in the few words that everyone signs.

Shen Bao Radio Weekly

Third Issue, Published Every Saturday

From Commercialization to Education 166

— Bi Jin

In the development of radio broadcasting, it can be divided into two periods. The first is the (commercialization) period, and the second is the (education) period. Only when the second period is reached does radio have true value for the public, and at the same time, radio itself can develop.

Currently, radio (commercialization) has reached its peak. The low price of radios makes them widely available to purchasers. Among those who install radios, stores are the largest majority, especially stores in urban areas, almost all of which have this new type of decoration. When you walk through bustling streets, in addition to the sounds of cars and trams, the loud music coming from the radio speakers of shops on both sides will make your ears deaf, and sometimes it will make you stop and listen. The radio itself has become the most fashionable advertising tool. If you own a radio, you can listen to the programs broadcast by various broadcasting stations continuously from morning to night. If you record what you hear, you will find a large amount of advertising. Whether it is in (storytelling with music), (songs), (folk tunes), or even in solemn speeches, almost all contain advertising components.

This situation is unavoidable in countries where the radio industry is still in its infancy, especially in countries where radio is commercialized. But I believe that one day this situation will end. In the future, the price of radios will be even lower, and more people will install them. At the same time, broadcasting stations will transition from (commercialization) to (popularization). At that time, the programs broadcast will change greatly with the renewal of public awareness. Many meaningless advertising programs will disappear, and in their place will be subjects that impart knowledge and entertainment that cultivates temperament. At that time, the radio industry will reach the (education) period, which is when it will have true value.

Ground Rod Resistance 167

— Xiao You

The resistance of the ground wire has a significant relationship to radio reception. This is something everyone has experienced. The usual method of grounding is to drive an iron or copper rod into the ground. This type of grounding is very convenient because it is easy to operate, the wiring can be done on the ground, and it can be driven deep into the ground to maintain moisture permanently.

This grounding method is most ideal if the length of the iron rod can reach the underground moisture layer (Moisture Level). This moisture layer varies depending on the geology of each location, but is mostly at a depth of eight to nine feet. If inserted shallowly, the resistance increases.

The above diagram shows the relationship between the depth of the ground rod and the resistance. From this diagram, it can be seen that the depth of the ground rod must be at least four feet.

In addition, the size, area, and number of ground rods are also related, but they are not very important. Also, even if there are many rods, if the distance between them is not more than three feet, the effect is even less. Beyond four rods, the efficiency cannot be increased any further.

Temporary Repair Method for Broken Headphone Wire 168

— VT

If the headphone wire is broken on the outside, it can be replaced with ordinary lamp wire without any difficulty. But if the internal coil is broken, it is not easy to repair the break yourself. Now there is a temporary solution. First, observe which coil is broken, and then connect the two ends of the broken coil together. Because there are often two coils inside the headphone, even if one is broken, the other can still be used. As shown in the figure, ABBC are the two coils inside the headphone. Assuming that the right coil is broken internally, then simply connect one end A to the point B where the two coils are connected with a wire, as shown by the dotted line. It will only sound slightly weaker.

Homemade Electromagnetic Phono Cartridge 169

— Zhen Zhi

Using an old headphone and some parts from a record player, you can make your own electromagnetic phono cartridge for testing audio frequency amplifiers (Audio Amplifier) and modulator systems (Modulator System).

The inside of the headphone does not need to be changed, just open a small hole in the back so that it can be mounted on a movable arm with a screw. As shown in the figure, connect the needle (Stylus) from the record player to the edge of the headphone, and weld the upper end to the center of the vibration diaphragm (DIAPh)ragm). The two ends of the electric wire inside the headphone are connected to the amplifier.

The arm for placing the cartridge is made of a long strip of brass. The screw connecting it to the cartridge should not be too tight, so that the cartridge can rotate freely on the turntable. At the other end, the support can be made of a brass tube, and a screw inserted into it to fix it to the base of the record player.

The frequency response of this cartridge is similar to that of ordinary headphones. Because its impedance (Linpedance) is extremely high, it is best used directly in the grid circuit of the first audio frequency amplification tube, or it can be passed through an ordinary amplification transformer. (Translated from OST)

Figures in the Radio World

Ampere 170

— KP

The discoverer of electromagnetic relations

Andre-Marie Ampere was French, born in Riom in 1775. His mathematical genius was evident in his early years. He did not have specialized study in science until after he married in 1799, when he specialized in the science necessary for educators in order to make a living. Throughout his life, his academic achievements were indeed quite great, and he made extraordinary contributions to the progress of science, especially in applying mathematical analysis to electromagnetic problems. In this respect, it is no exaggeration to call him a pioneer of radio. His research results seem to have paved the way for the later British physicist Michael Faraday (1791-1867). After hearing about Oersted's discovery, he immediately began experiments. In 1820, he had already established the law concerning the movement of a magnetic needle with the direction of the current, and later discovered extremely important phenomena such as the fact that coils have magnetic force when current is flowing through them. He died in 1836.

Joyful to the Point of Losing Oneself 171

Radio Common Sense 172

— Wei

(3) Electron Flow - Electric Current

The electric lights, telephones, telegraphs, electric stoves, etc. that we use every day all utilize electric current. As mentioned above, radio waves are also generated by the vibration of electric current. So, what exactly is electric current? We must first understand this.

According to recent scientists' research, any substance is composed of only two things: one is called an electron (Electron), and the other is called a nucleus (Nucleus). Electrons revolve around the nucleus in various numbers. The situation is similar to the Earth and planets revolving around the sun. Because of the different numbers of electrons, various kinds of atoms are formed. Any molecule or atom has a fixed number of electrons. It cannot have one more or one less. If it loses one, it must use great force to replenish it. If it has one more, it cannot be stable and must get rid of it. No matter how far away, as long as there is a path, they will quickly link together to make up for deficiencies. The speed of their movement is almost the speed of light. This is how electric current is formed.

When a substance has more electrons, it develops a special property called negative electricity, also called negative charge; when it lacks electrons, it also develops a special property called positive electricity, also called positive charge. The electron is the smallest thing in the world, and its mass is only about one eighteen-hundredth of that of a light atom. It often exists in large numbers in various metals, called free electrons. These electrons all have a negative charge, and usually move freely within the metal body, scattered without a fixed direction. But once they come into contact with something with a positive charge, they flow endlessly towards it to combine with it. (Electrons repel each other.) After combining, they no longer function. This is called neutralization. Therefore, if we want to generate electric current, we just need to find a way to make the electrons inside the metal body move. For example, if we apply voltage to both ends of a metal wire, the electrons will flow in a certain direction, forming an electric current. However, the direction of the current generally referred is exactly opposite to the direction of electron flow. It is said that current flows freely from the positive electrode to the negative electrode. Any metal body or other substance that easily conducts electric current is called a conductor.

The magnitude of the electric current is the amount of electrons or charged molecules (such molecules are scientifically called ions (Ion)) flowing. The amount of this flow depends on the needs at the two ends of the conductor and the ease of flow. This can also be compared to water. Fill a bottle with water and open a hole at the bottom, connecting a tube. The water will flow out of the tube. If the water level in the bottle is very high, then the water flow will be rapid and large. This is because a high water pressure means a large water flow. Also, if the hole or the connected tube has a larger diameter, then the resistance decreases, and the water flow increases. The same is true for electric current. The needs are explained by the word voltage (Voltage). A high voltage will cause the current to increase. At the same time, if the resistance to current flow is high, for example, if the conductor is a thin wire or other substance that does not easily conduct electricity, then the current decreases. This is called resistance (Resistance).

The relationship between these three factors, current, voltage, and resistance, can be defined by Ohm's law. This will be discussed later.

Page 16

Shen Bao Fourth Sheet

Units of Electricity (1) 173

— Jun

(1) Unit of Current Intensity

The quantity that expresses the degree of strength of an electric current is called current intensity. The unit of current intensity is called ampere (Ampere). The value of one ampere is the current intensity of a constant current that, when passed through a silver nitrate solution, can deposit 0.001118 grams of silver per second.

There are two other units for measuring smaller currents:

(Symbol mA) = one thousandth of an ampere

(Symbol uA) = one hundred thousandth of an ampere

Current is often represented by the letter 丨 in formulas.

(2) Unit of Electric Charge

Electric currents have strengths, due to the number of electric charges passing through the wires per second. This number of electric charges is called electric charge. The unit of electric charge is called coulomb (Coulomb), and its value is the amount of electric charge that one ampere of current passes through any cross-section of a wire in one second. Electric charge is represented by the letter Q in formulas.

One coulomb contains 6.29 io i8 electrons. Therefore, in practice, one ampere is the rate of flow of 6.29 io i8 electrons passing through a point in a circuit per second.

A larger unit of electric charge is called (ampere-hour). One ampere-hour is equal to 3600 coulombs.

Reader Research

My Homemade Single-Tube Radio 175

— Jia Ming

I admit I am a not-so-ambitious radio enthusiast. Now everyone tends towards AC power, while I still linger with DC; now everyone is expanding to three or four tubes, while I still stick to a single tube. I am becoming more and more outdated, but I have also evolved: from the non-power-consuming crystal radio to the slightly power-consuming single-tube radio.

During the (broadcasting era of the Kairo Company), I curiously made a crystal radio to play with, but being naturally restless, I kept dismantling and tinkering with it, considering it research. Finally, because it was only a crystal radio, it could not satisfy my curiosity, so I resolved to make a single-tube radio. At first, I didn't achieve much, but later, after disassembling and reassembling, modifying left and right, and working diligently on the single-tube radio for several years, I actually came up with a method that I considered satisfactory. It was just that I myself felt satisfied. As for whether the method is reasonable or not! Or even if it is already very outdated and not worth a look from experts, that is unknown. But what is worth boasting about is: easy to manufacture, economical, long reception range, and pleasing sound.

Now, let's publish the circuit diagram as follows:

The above method is said to be regenerative, that is, it has two stages of amplification, high frequency and low frequency. The materials used are very ordinary. If you are just starting out, you should first purchase the following items:

One UX201A vacuum tube

One Ux vacuum tube socket

Two ·00035 capacitors

One 25 resistor

One 5:1 variable condenser

One fixed crystal (with mount) (I used Carboraindum)

One roll of #24 double silk-covered wire

Four binding posts

One 6VA storage battery

One 90V B battery

One 4.5V C battery

Two three-inch dials

One spiderweb coil frame (with board)

Three feet of connecting wire

One 4000-ohm headphone (I used Telefunken)

One hundred feet of antenna wire

Forty or fifty feet of ground wire (rubber insulated wire)

One piece of bakelite

One baseboard

Several round-head screws

One small wooden box

Two antenna insulators

Now let me tell you how to make my single-tube radio:

First, wind 60 turns of #24 double silk-covered wire (Li) on the spiderweb coil frame, then add another 20 turns (L) outside the Li coil on the same board. Wind the regenerative coil (12) on another spiderweb board, also with twenty turns. Then, according to the above two diagrams, connect the wires according to the diagram. The shorter the wiring, the better, and the arrangement should be neat and beautiful.

After all the wiring is completely in place, you should first check whether the wiring is incorrect, especially paying attention to the incorrect connection of the A and B batteries. If it is completely correct, good results are guaranteed. Because this machine uses a crystal detector and a 201A amplifier, it is perfectly suitable.

However, it may be that due to slight differences in location and wiring procedures, the sound reception efficiency may be reduced (or it may even be strengthened, it's hard to say), which should be taken into account by the assembler. If you feel that the reception range is not far enough, the detection is not sensitive, or the sound reception is noisy, you can raise or shorten the antenna, or add a ·10000 variable capacitor in the antenna circuit; if the regeneration is too strong, you can separate the Lx12 coils very far. These should naturally follow general rules.

Later, I changed the A battery of this machine to AC power. Although the results were worse than DC, it saved a lot of trouble such as charging. Let me talk about it next time when I have the opportunity.

Page 18

Free Talk

Talking about Promotional Texts 193

— Yu Dafu

In China, the promotional effect of words has always been considered very important. Reading a proclamation can cure headaches, spreading a proclamation can stabilize the Jiangnan region, and those who kill thieves on horseback and write official reports after dismounting are considered to be all-round talents in both civil and military affairs. Sweeping with a sharp pen can sweep away 5,000 people. In modern times, the use of this textual propaganda has become even more widespread. Shops that specialize in selling Japanese goods will post leaflets vowing not to buy or sell enemy goods, and even beggars who tear up advertising paper to make clothes are wearing large characters saying "Aviation Saves the Country." Furthermore, not long ago, Rehe had won many victories, and after the September 18th Incident, the volunteer army killed enemies, and it is unknown how many tens of thousands they killed.

In the past few days, the situation has changed, and even the words "shortening the line of defense" and "luring the enemy deep" in the newspapers feel outdated. So, they have become declarations. They say, "The direct negotiations reported outside are not true." Then they say, "If the Japanese invaders enter south of the Great Wall, our army will resist to the death, and the responsibility should be borne by Japan." Even the distant Guangdong Province in the southwest has issued orders to store grain and defend against insults, and the dock workers in Shanghai have issued a declaration welcoming Wang Jingwei to save the country.

These are all very good promotional texts, which can suppress people's hearts to a great extent, and can also bluff and bluster to a small extent. However, if the bluffing becomes too excessive, there is also a danger of becoming unable to justify oneself later. The Japanese have a saying, called (笛聲徹天，踊者不前), which Japanese newspapers often use to mock us. In fact, we are indeed a little qualified to be mocked. However, our ancestors also had some foresight. They had long seen that these textual propagandas created by them would definitely become empty signboards that would deceive both the old and the young. Therefore, they left us a final word, called (有文事者必有武備). "Those who engage in civil affairs must have military preparations!" I repeat this sentence here again, so that the Japanese soldiers will not underestimate us too much, and just kill their way into the city.

March 17, 1933

Liu Zongyuan Demands that Hu Huaichen Correct and Apologize 194

— Xiaofeng

Today, I feel slightly unwell. I lay in bed in the morning and read "Free Talk," and I still fell asleep in a daze. My deceased friend suddenly came in a dream, saying that he had just met Liu Zongyuan (Why hasn't Liu Zongyuan been reincarnated yet? I can't explain this, I have to ask Mr. Hu Huaichen, who has been a vegetarian for ten years and wholeheartedly worships Buddha). Zongyuan was very angry, saying that Hu Huaichen (arbitrarily) tampered with his articles, (damaging his personal reputation, he must demand correction and apology). He attached a letter and entrusted him to forward it to me and introduce it to "Free Talk" for publication, so that he could follow the example (publish this letter, and automatically correct and apologize.) Dead people also want to settle accounts with the living, which is really troublesome! But since I have been entrusted, I have to copy the letter and send it out. Whether or not it is published depends on the editor's example. The original letter is as follows:

To Mr. Li Liewen, Editor of Free Talk: Today I saw in the "Free Talk" published on March 16 (Letters to the Editor, one knows that Hu Huaichen thinks that his articles are very authoritative and does not allow others to comment. If there are any comments, he must automatically correct and apologize. If this example is implemented, then he should also do the same to others. Now I find in my humble work (Records of the Mountains and Rivers of Liuzhou Near the Administration that Can Be Visited,):" (石魚之山全石，無大草木，山小而高，其形如立魚，在多秭歸西) in one sentence he arbitrarily tampered with it without giving any reason. He crossed out my original word (在) with square brackets, and also put (西) at the beginning of the next sentence. (See (Student Chinese Classics Series) published by the Commercial Press (Liu Zongyuan's Works, page 194). He arbitrarily tampered with it, making my article inconsistent. Also, on page 76 of the same book, in the article (Records of the You Huangjin Stream), because I had already mentioned the Huangjin Temple in front, and then described the Huangjin Temple above, I omitted the word (祠) and wrote (黄神), saying: (黄神之上，揭水八十步，···.) He also arbitrarily ridiculed the two words (黄神), saying (the word 神 is suspected to be a mistake for the word 祠). Since he arbitrarily ridicules and tampers with it like this, I now believe that there is a need to follow the example (to demand correction and apology). The simple explanation is as follows:

(1) My first sentence, in today's fashionable language, is to use the product to represent the place of origin. This writing style was commonly used by ancient people, and it was even more commonly used in the Overseas Classic in the (Classic of Mountains and Seas.) This sentence imitates the writing style of (Classic of Mountains and Seas), using the three words (多秭歸) to represent the Xianyi Mountain in Duozigui mentioned in the previous article. He repeatedly said that I was studying (Classic of Mountains and Seas), but he did not (carefully check (Classic of Mountains and Seas) to see if there was such a writing style, and arbitrarily tampered with it, and arbitrarily added a note, saying (this sentence Duozigui refers to the Mountain of Stone Fish being Duozigui.) And he deliberately compiled it into the (Student Chinese Classics Series,) widely publicizing it to the student community. I believe that it damages my personal reputation and must demand correction and apology.

(2) My second sentence is also a commonly used abbreviation. I can't remember many examples at the moment, but I remember reading a book about my world that has such a sentence:

The residence bestowed by Duke Qiu Wenda is at the Stone Tiger in Xuanwumen: Before Wenda: it was the Right Wing Zongxue: Before the Zongxue, it was the residence of Prince Wu: Before Prince Wu, it was the residence of Zhou Yanru, a senior scholar of the former Ming Dynasty.

This book is (Notes from the Thatched Cottage of Reading the Subtle) by Ji Yun of the Qing Dynasty. The sentence quoted can be found in (As I Heard) 4. There are two omissions like mine in the sentence: one is the omission of the (First word) after (Before Wenda) of (Wenda), and the other is the omission of the (Residence) character after (Before Prince Wu) of (Prince Wu). He also arbitrarily ridiculed my abbreviation and promoted it in the student community. I believe that it also damages my personal reputation and must demand correction and apology.

(3) My request is made according to precedent, and I am not deliberately fooling around. Please publish this letter so that he will not think that there is no proof of death and he can say anything arbitrarily.

Sincerely, I wish you peace. From Liu Zongyuan, March 16

Counterattack 195

— He Dian

You Eastern foreign devils are too bullying. Do you want to take three provinces and then four? Okay, if you want to strip off my outer coat, I'll give you my underwear too. If you want to slap me on my left cheek, I'll give you my right cheek too. We are truly a long-established, dignified country of etiquette. Taking a tooth for a tooth and an eye for an eye is not acceptable. Are you going to make our father angry enough to take out a machine gun to fight back? A weasel will have a life-saving fart to push back if it is chased too hard. Have you seen the speech our father made?

This time I will definitely resist resolutely and without mercy.

Wait a minute, wait until I get on the plane before you start shelling.

It's okay to defend Rehe for ten days.

What's more, Tang Yulin was wanted for his lack of effort in defending.

You little ones are too proud and simply don't know what's good for you.

You occupied Rehe, Gubeikou, Xifengkou and took the Great Wall.

If you insist on advancing, our father has plenty of long-term resistance. Haven't you seen in the newspapers that our army is going to counterattack? And look, the non-resistance general has already telegraphed his resignation. Resist, resist, the third one is still resist, we are determined.

Do you know that our father has also mobilized hundreds of thousands of troops to suppress a few bandits?

How can we say that there are no large troops to deal with you, the robber who is invading us?

I advise you to clean up Rehe quickly and hold a celebration meeting.

Our father will catch his breath so that he can launch another round of counter-attacks.

Long Creative Work

The Crossroads of Era and Love 196

— Zhang Guanping

Mr. Zhu masked his shame with a joking tone.

The public bus arrived. Haiquan and Mr. Zhu Wei boarded the bus together, sharing a seat.

"Are you going to school too?"

"No. I need to take a few days off."

"Why?"

"My grandfather passed away."

Haiquan casually made up this lie. In fact, his grandfather had been dead for seven or eight years.

"Oh, I am sorry..."

Mr. Zhu said this English sentence, which aroused Haiquan's resentment. He thought, Mr. Zhu has never been to the United States or the Dutch, so why is he saying British words so playfully? At most, he is just a graduate of the English specialization department of a church school in Nanjing. "Then you're not going back?"

"I'm not going back."

Haiquan shook his head.

"Mr. Lin, if you don't go back, it's better to go to class. No one can avoid death! How old was your grandfather this year?"

"About seventy-one or seventy-two years old, I guess."

"That's about it..."

Haiquan found Mr. Zhu's nodding expression very ridiculous, and wanted to laugh, but quickly held back.

"Mr. Lin, have you heard any news at school?"

After a while, Zhu Wei suddenly asked Haiquan in a different way.

"(No.)"

Haiquan was also a little surprised and stared at Professor Zhu's face. He saw a yellow particle, between solid and liquid, hanging on the corner of Mr. Zhu's left eye. He then thought, Mr. Zhu hasn't even wiped his face clean, and he's saying "I am sorry"?

"Mr. Lin, you have to help me."

Running Backwards 197

— Zhang Menglin

What is the same rhyme? I asked an old gentleman from Qiu, who teaches Chinese at school.

"If a person uses a rhyme foot of 'yu', and you use it as your rhyme foot as well, that's called 'matching the rhyme.'" The old gentleman said.

"So, what if he not only takes someone else's foot, but even takes someone else's half body?" I had not yet finished speaking.

"Does he want to become that person?" The old gentleman asked.

"No, he wants to turn that person into himself."

"I mean, if he doesn't just use one rhyme foot, but uses two or three words, is it right to claim that this is a matching rhyme?" I asked again.

"Such a claim." The old gentleman brought up the past, and said with emotion. "In the past, when taking the imperial examination to become a Xiucai, one would be punished." "How would they be punished?"

"At that time, for a Xiucai who made such a claim, we would give him a fourth-class examination and punish him to carry a red manure bucket, meaning we would tell him to support the teacher."

"Ah, this gentleman is indeed studying agriculture, and I think he probably got a fourth-class grade at school."

"Oh, everything is going backwards now," the old gentleman sighed for a while.

But this solved a problem for me. Mr. Boyu, a student of the Agricultural University, said in a certain tabloid that two poems by a Mr. Zhang used three or four words from other people in each sentence, which was in accordance with the original rhyme. And he said, "But I admire his poems. His poems have a kind of fresh and passionate emotion..." If you haven't smelled the manure bucket, you won't be able to tell the difference between fragrance and foulness.

Coffin Shop 198

— Cao Juren

Suzhou Short Stay Diary Two

Suzhou is full of...? (Suzhou is full of beauties!)

I don't think so. (Shanghai has more beauties than Suzhou.) Suzhou has the most coffin shops. They are everywhere on the streets and alleys. Outside the city of Suzhou, there are new stone monuments of the Suzhou Cemetery Protection Association everywhere. Since cemeteries can be protected, then coffin shops should be opened more, which should be logical. The president of the Cemetery Protection Association is said to be a highly respected (Mr. Peng, a local worthy); it would be even more appropriate if he also served as the boss of a coffin shop (the right person in the right place). Having a cup of tea, chatting casually, and passing the rest of your life in this way, the people of Suzhou seem not to be attached to the world. They only care about coffins, and if fir wood is not enough, they use nanmu; if nanmu is not enough, they use agarwood. For tombs, if soil mounds are not enough, they use stone enclosures; if stone enclosures are not enough, they use cemetery protection associations. It's all about the flavor of drinking tea and chatting leisurely. It makes me a little confused. Someone said: Most of the people who live in Suzhou as rentiers are old men with declining years. They don't have many days left to live, so they treat Suzhou as a large cemetery and make arrangements for the next life everywhere. This is closer to the truth. However, the wilderness is still the wilderness, undulating in height, and only a foot high; the coffins turn into dung, and the corpses turn into worms. It still takes the strength of Mr. Peng to prevent them from becoming a flat ground. If you understand it with the philosophy of drinking tea and chatting leisurely, then there is no need to open coffin shops, no need to set up cemetery protection associations, and Mr. Peng would also feel that everything is superfluous. It's a pity that these words can't be said to the people of Suzhou.

The streets and alleys of Suzhou are full of black walls; black symbolizes death, and this color is quite harmonious with coffin shops. As soon as I see black walls, I think I'm walking into a tomb. At that time, I was reading various records of the Russian Soviet Union's five-year plan; the Russian Soviet Union regarded wood as very precious, and using it for firewood would be considered a waste of good material. But I myself was living in a circle of bosses who planned to bury the single-width fir wood underground to let it rot. It's really (living next to ghosts)! Listen, Suzhou dialect is coming:

(Where do you live?)

(I live next to a coffin shop.)

(That's really bad luck!)

Page 19

Luo Wengan Returns to Beijing 208

In order to safeguard the nation's and the people's survival, as well as territorial sovereignty and integrity, our country has no choice but to resist in self-defense.
