Before the lost territories are recovered, direct negotiations would be akin to a surrender under duress. I dare say that our country's diplomacy will never be subdued by Japan's violence. We will continue to resist to the end, seeking survival through struggle."

Japanese Consulate Detectives 209

Arrest Three Korean Revolutionaries

Seized three pistols and two bombs on the spot. The three Koreans were plotting to assassinate Japanese envoy Arichika Akira

Several people were also arrested in conjunction with the French police and Chinese police

The "China Press" reports: At 9:25 last night, secret detectives from the Japanese Consulate in this port, in conjunction with the Hongkou police, arrested three Koreans at the Song Jiang Chun Restaurant, No. 271 Wuchang Road. Three pistols and two bombs were seized. The method of manufacture was the same as that used in the Hongkou Park bombing last year that killed General Shirakawa, among others. It is reported that the three Koreans will be charged with plotting to assassinate Japanese envoy Arichika Akira. The three are Li Kangxun, 22 years old; Bai Jiubo, 28 years old; and Xuan Xun. It is believed that they recently threw a bomb at the Japanese Consulate in Tianjin. They were caught off guard and could not resist arrest, so they surrendered. It is reported that these three, along with a person in Western attire, went to the restaurant together last night, but the person in Western attire left after talking briefly at the bottom of the stairs and did not go upstairs. Last night, detectives searched for this person, but his whereabouts were still unknown when the "China Press" went to print. Previously, the Japanese Consulate received a confidential report stating that some Koreans were planning to assassinate Japanese envoy Arichika Akira last night. The Japanese envoy was attending a banquet at a certain Japanese hall on Peng Road that night. Secret detectives were stationed all around, patrolling the area. They saw a suspicious person enter the Song Jiang Chun Restaurant and secretly went to surround and arrest him. At a signal, they rushed upstairs in a crowd. All the people were wearing steel mesh vests, so they were even bolder. When they went upstairs, they saw the three Koreans sitting at a table, just about to start eating. Before they could move, they were seized by the crowd. They were disarmed, and a package resembling a lunchbox was placed aside. Inside were two bombs, one square, weighing about five pounds, and one smaller and round, both made in the same way. According to the Japanese authorities' examination last night, they felt that they were made by Europeans. In order to eliminate Korean reactionary parties, Japanese police and Hongkou police detectives, in conjunction with French Concession police and Nanshi police, searched various suspected locations. Two of the arrested people resided at No. 16 Laishi Road, near Xujiahui Road. The detectives went to the address to search, and as a result, they obtained information and went to other locations to search. For a while, patrol cars were dispatched in all directions. The result was unknown late at night. It is reported that several people were arrested. The three Koreans arrested at the Song Jiang Chun Restaurant were first taken to the Hongkou Police Station. After completing the procedures, they were transferred to the Japanese authorities. It is reported that many Korean revolutionaries have secretly arrived in Shanghai in recent weeks.

A representative of the "China Press" rushed to the Song Jiang Chun Restaurant to inquire a few minutes after the incident. According to the restaurant staff, just after 9 o'clock, two Chinese people, one dressed in Western attire, leisurely went upstairs. A few minutes later, two more Western-dressed guests arrived in rickshaws and stood near the stairs, talking in a low voice, unable to hear what they were saying, and unable to distinguish their dialect. Before long, one of those standing went away. The remaining one went upstairs and joined the two who had arrived earlier and were sitting by the window. The three ordered a bottle of beer and a plate of fried fish. They spoke in Northern dialect, and one of them spoke Chinese very fluently, but their appearance was still Korean. At first, I didn't pay attention to what the three were carrying. After I poured wine into three cups, they finished it in a few minutes. I went downstairs to urge the kitchen to quickly serve the fried fish, and I saw several unusual people looking around in front of the restaurant. A waiter wanted to go out for something, but was blocked by a Westerner in uniform. Looking at the back door, there were also several people in steel mesh vests guarding there. They were not Westerners. I can be sure that they were all Japanese. When the fried fish was served, the three were just about to pick up their chopsticks when people in steel mesh vests rushed upstairs with shields and pistols. There were at least eight Japanese who went upstairs, but I didn't have time to count them. In addition, there was one Western police chief and one Chinese detective. As soon as these people went upstairs, they pointed their guns at the three. I was very surprised, but the three did not change their expressions, did not jump up, and did not even lift their hands. The police searched the three, and I was pushed to the back of the crowd. Later, I heard that they had found two pistols, but I didn't see them. I only saw a small package wrapped in newspaper on the table. At that time, there was still one Chinese diner at another table, and after being checked, he was also pushed to the back of the crowd. What surprised me most was that the three customers were calm throughout and always had smiles on their faces. One of them, dressed in a Chinese long robe, even laughed loudly when the Japanese police patted his cheek. The three were then taken away by the crowd. I didn't see if they got into a car. The three were between 25 and 35 years old. The one who left earlier never returned.

MacDonald Arrives in Rome 219

Meetings with Mussolini Today and Tomorrow. The Japanese Military's Attitude Toward British Disarmament.

Havas, Geneva, 17th - British Prime Minister MacDonald and Foreign Minister Simon departed from here for Italy at 8:45 this evening. According to sources in Rome, Italian figures believe that in these turbulent international times, it is very gratifying that British authorities have come to Rome to discuss plans for the construction of Europe with the Italian government. They believe that this meeting has a major relationship with Europe and Italy.

Havas, Rome, 17th - British Prime Minister MacDonald and Foreign Minister Simon traveled by train from Geneva to Genoa, Italy, and then switched to an airplane personally piloted by Italian Air Minister General Balbo to fly to Rome. When the plane arrived in the capital, Prime Minister Mussolini personally went to the airport to welcome MacDonald and Simon. The two went directly from the airport to the British Embassy for lunch. After lunch, they held talks. In the evening, Mussolini hosted a banquet. On Sunday, MacDonald toured Rome and continued talks in the afternoon. There was also an evening banquet at the British Embassy.

United Press, Tokyo, 8th - Regarding the new disarmament plan proposed by British Prime Minister MacDonald on the 6th, the Army authorities will study the contents after the report arrives. The opinions they currently hold on the various proposals are roughly as follows: The new proposal stipulates that the longest service period for combat personnel is eight months. This is a proposal for European countries and has nothing to do with Japan. If the proposal applies to countries outside of Europe, Japan's service period is one and a half years, so it is very difficult to train soldiers in such a short period of time, and the required expenses are also considerable. Japan cannot agree. The plan also stipulates that Germany's troop numbers are 200,000, which France will definitely not recognize, which is clear. Japan cannot agree to limiting the caliber of mobile land artillery to 150 millimeters, but the maximum limit of 16 inches for coastal defense artillery is acceptable. The maximum weight of tanks being 16 tons is a plan that is beneficial to Britain. France advocates for 60 tons, and Japan advocates for 25 tons. Also, the military aircraft of France, Japan, Italy, Russia, the United States, and Britain are limited to 500 aircraft, which Japan absolutely cannot agree to. It is difficult to distinguish between military and civilian aircraft. Britain and the United States have 20 times more civilian aircraft than Japan, so equal regulations should not be applied.

Havas, Hungarian Capital, 17th - The Cabinet will hold an extraordinary State Council meeting tomorrow, chaired by Regent Admiral Horthy. The Hungarian Chief Representative to the Disarmament Conference, Tang Zuo Si, will also attend in order to discuss Hungary's attitude towards British Prime Minister MacDonald's disarmament proposal. Responsible individuals are extremely impressed with the situation of the Geneva consultation and the talks between the British and Italian Prime Ministers in Rome. They seem to be quite supportive of MacDonald's disarmament plan.

Havas, Geneva, 17th - Today, Disarmament Conference Chairman Henderson invited French Prime Minister Daladier to lunch. Most of the heads of delegations and important figures currently in Geneva, such as Czech Foreign Minister Benes, US Disarmament Representative Gibson, French Foreign Minister Boncour, and British Foreign Secretary Simon, were invited. The Disarmament Conference's Armaments Committee has adjourned indefinitely, as has the Aviation Committee.

Japan Announces Withdrawal from the League of Nations Nears 220

Dentong, Tokyo, 18th - The Privy Council's review of the consultation case on withdrawing from the League of Nations was virtually completed yesterday. This afternoon, the committee of the Privy Council (the government side did not participate) will exchange opinions and decide on its attitude towards the consultation case, which will be presented to the Privy Council's plenary meeting on the 23rd. It is hoped that it will be unanimously approved. After approval, Prime Minister Saito and Foreign Minister Uchida will jointly enter the palace that afternoon to report to the Emperor and obtain his approval. Then, Foreign Minister Uchida will send the full text by telegram to the League of Nations Imperial Affairs Bureau in Geneva. Director of the Imperial Affairs Bureau, Sawada, will hand it over to Secretary-General Drummond. Therefore, the notification of withdrawal will be on the 22nd, or at the latest on the 23rd. At the same time, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs will issue a notice and statement.

Japanese Army and Navy Wear Silk Shirts 221

Americans Don't Buy Japanese Raw Silk. Japanese Use Silk to Make Their Own Shirts.

Reuters, London, 17th - Lister & Co., textile merchants from Bradford, England, issued a notice today stating that the shirts worn by Japanese army and navy soldiers are now made of silk. Japan is the world's largest producer of raw silk, and the United States is the largest consumer of raw silk. However, at present, American trade is very sluggish. Japan is unwilling to sell all of its silk on the market, which would result in a sharp drop in market prices. Therefore, it weaves its own silk goods, and then uses silk to make shirts for army and navy soldiers.

At this time, opinions will also be exchanged on the issue of his future. Therefore, the Prime Minister's actions after the Diet are extremely noteworthy.

Colombia-Peru Dispute 223

League of Nations Drafts Recommendation

Report Evidence, Wrongdoing Lies with Peru. Recommend Troop Withdrawal, Reopen Negotiations.

Reuters, Geneva, 17th - Today, the Council of the League of Nations, regarding the dispute between Colombia and Peru, has drafted a report in the precedent of the Sino-Japanese dispute. The content of the report includes historical facts, conclusions, and recommendations. The evidence cited in this report is unfavorable to Peru and recommends that both parties immediately withdraw their troops from the disputed area and begin negotiations. For months, Peru and Colombia have been fighting an undeclared war over Leticia, a small town on the Amazon River.

Guangzhou: Although industry and commerce in this region have been affected by the global economic decline, and the situation in North China has caused unease, Guangzhou's municipal development has not been slowed. Arrest of British Citizens in Moscow Incident 234

Tense Anglo-Soviet Relations

Litvinov Insists Foreigners Must Be Subject to Soviet Law. British Ambassador Protests, Saying Anglo-Soviet Relations Are at the Point of Rupture

Reuters, Moscow, 17th - Soviet Foreign Minister Litvinov notified the British Ambassador in Moscow today that the employees of the arrested Vickers Electrical Company will be tried in the Supreme Court on charges of counter-revolution. The punishment for this crime is the death penalty. Litvinov refuted the notion that British citizens residing in the Soviet Union are not subject to Soviet law. Litvinov expressed hope that this case would not affect Anglo-Soviet relations, as relations are more important than any store or individual. The British Ambassador to Russia has protested, saying that the charge of sabotage is not credible and demanding that the case be dropped, otherwise it will affect the Anglo-Soviet trade agreement that expires on July 17, and Anglo-Soviet relations may be at the point of rupture.

Reuters, Moscow, 17th - Litvinov said this afternoon that no sense of oppression or threat can make Soviet law lax or release the arrested British citizens. If the British government and the British Ambassador both believe that the arrested are innocent, then their panic about the fate of the arrested is incomprehensible. The case will be publicly tried in the Supreme Court within one month.

Feng consistently advocates national mobilization for resisting Japan and saving the country. Li represents the Central Government to discuss the entire anti-Japanese plan with Feng

Fujian 238

Plan to Reorganize the People's Militia

The Provincial Government Establishes the Militia Affairs Office to Oversee Militia Affairs Throughout the Province

Fuzhou Dispatch: Due to inconvenient transportation between the province and its districts and the complexity of the situations in various places, the organization of the people's militia is unsystematic, leading to local bullies and ruffians using the name of the militia to carry out exploitation and extortion, even looting, arson, and murder, turning it into a class that oppresses the people. The provincial government, being recently aware of this, has decided to reorganize the people's militia and has specially established a Militia Affairs Office to oversee militia affairs throughout the province. Chiang Guangnai will concurrently serve as the director of the office. Under him, there will be one secretary, and it will be divided into two sections. The first section will have three groups: design, personnel, and propaganda. The second section will have two groups: management and general affairs. Several inspectors will also be appointed to supervise and inspect the progress of militia affairs in various counties. The first step of the office's plan is to change the current system of recruiting soldiers, so that militiamen are all filled by good citizens, who can be a strong army when gathered and still be farmers and workers when scattered. The "Provisional Regulations for the Fujian Provincial Defense Regiment" have been drafted and submitted to the provincial government for approval and implementation. The method is to divide the province into ten defense regiment districts, each with a chief and deputy commander, governing several counties (roughly from four or five to six or seven counties). Each county will also have a chief and deputy commander, and several standing squads will be established based on local conditions (roughly from two to four squads). Each squad will be divided into three platoons, and each platoon will be divided into three sections, with ten people in each section. All men aged 20 to 40 who have resided in the county for more than one year should be incorporated into the county's defense regiment and be obligated to undergo training and service. The term of service for the standing squad is nine months, after which they will be transferred to the reserve squad. The term of service for the reserve squad is two years and three months, after which they will be transferred to the rear guard squad. The term of service for the rear guard squad will be up to the age of military service. According to the office's plan, after this system is implemented for five years, the total number of people in the standing, reserve, and rear guard squads in the province can reach more than 1.71 million, all of whom have undergone military training and can be summoned at any time. In order to cultivate cadre talents, a militia cadre training institute will be specially established. The director of the institute will be concurrently held by the director of the Militia Affairs Office, and a director will be appointed under him, concurrently held by the secretary of the Militia Affairs Office, to preside over all affairs of the institute. It will be divided into primary and advanced classes. Primary students will be recommended by various counties from graduates of secondary schools or above, who are qualified with pure thoughts and healthy bodies, with five to twelve people from each county, totaling about 500 people. The advanced class will recruit retired military officers and those with military knowledge, totaling more than 100 people, and will be taught various knowledge of military affairs, politics, militia affairs, and society. Both classes are scheduled to graduate in four months. After graduation, they will be assigned to work in militia organizations at all levels. The primary class has been open for more than a month, and the advanced class will also begin on March 1. The office is also afraid that the people will not fully understand the reorganization at the beginning of its implementation and that obstacles will occur in the progress, so it has expanded propaganda and defined two items: propaganda steps and propaganda areas. The first phase of propaganda will publicize the theory of running the militia, the second phase will publicize the practical methods of running the militia, and the third phase will publicize the theory and practice of businesses related to the defense regiment (such as improving rural production, afforestation movement, cooperative businesses, etc.). The areas, in addition to those that are extremely common and superficial and do not contain local characteristics, will strive to be practical and consistent with the actual local situation, in order to arouse the interest of the people and create the concept of their support and assistance. Various pamphlets, leaflets, and pictorials have been compiled and printed and distributed to various counties for distribution. In order to make the people understand the practical measures of the militia in the future and to set an example for practical results, Minhou County, the provincial capital, has been designated as the Fujian Provincial Defense Regiment Experimental County and will be the first to implement the new system. A special commissioner has been dispatched by the office to cooperate with the Minhou County government to prepare for it. (March 10)

Japanese Privy Council Thinks Diplomacy Failed 239

Uchida Should Bear Full Responsibility

The Tokyo Asahi Shimbun reported that the cabinet decision on the League of Nations withdrawal case was made on the 11th, but it must be reviewed by the Privy Council. Currently, the review committee consists of nine members, including Chairman Kuratomi, with Heiji Kiichiro as the chairman. However, the Privy Council believes that: (1) Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations, because it could not carry out its主張, resulted in a score of forty-two to one, which cannot be said to be a major diplomatic failure; (2) Those who suffered this major failure must be blamed on the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. Therefore, Foreign Minister Uchida should bear full responsibility for the failure; (3) After withdrawing from the League of Nations, it is also doubtful whether the Japanese government has a solid diplomatic fundamental policy. Strict responsibility will be pursued regarding the above three points.

Ridiculous and Absurd 247

Schemes of the Tyrannical Japan

The Sino-Federal Empire Secret Agreement Will Further Disrupt Our Country, Support Rebels to Enter the Pass and Restore the Dynasty

The tyrannical Japan has occupied Northeast China and Jehol, and its ambitions have not yet ended. It is constantly spying on and disrupting Tianjin and Peking. Recently, there have been rumors that Japan and the puppet regime have signed a secret agreement (the Sino-Federal Empire Secret Agreement). After many inquiries, its ridiculous and absurd plan has been obtained, which is urgently disclosed as follows:

(1) There are only two types of countries in the world today: one is capitalist, such as Britain, the United States, Japan, Italy, and France, and the other is communist, such as Soviet Russia. Now, to resist Soviet Russia, China and Japan must unite, and then persuade Britain, the United States, Italy, and France to understand its practices, which cannot be successful. (2) To unite China and Japan, Japan must not assist Manchuria, restore the imperial system, and eliminate the Chinese Communist Party and the Kuomintang, which once united with the Communists. A major problem cannot be successful. (3) According to historical research, there are three ways to pacify the world: one is a popular movement, one is military conquest, and one is historical evolution and popular elections. China has already gone bankrupt and cannot be applied. Military conquest has passed through Yuan Shikai, Xu Shichang, Duan Qirui, and Chiang Kai-shek, all of whom have failed and cannot be successful. Now, after more than 300 years, the Emperor Xuantong can win over a group of people and can apply the dictatorship system to sort out all the plans of the new country. China wants to unite with Japan, and Japan must help the Emperor of the Sino-Federal Empire restore power to be successful. To help the Emperor restore power, the first step is to recover North China as the basic country. Second, we must imitate the method of the Qin State helping Chong'er of the Jin State restore the country, the method of Britain and France helping Poland, Turkey, and other small European countries gain independence, and the method of France helping the United States break away from Britain. Formal army, navy, and air force forces must be used to eliminate the Communist Party and the Kuomintang, which once tolerated the Communists. Third, the Chinese people are poor and have exhausted their wealth, which has reached its extreme. Japan must first provide economic assistance to sort out the army, banks, and other relief measures, and then turn to other countries to raise public debt, build railways, develop mines, reclaim wasteland, and revitalize various industries. If these three points of assistance are possible, the Sino-Japanese Alliance can be successful. If Japan is willing to help the Sino-Federal Empire restore power, it must obtain the area north of the Yellow River as the foundation. To obtain the provinces north of the Yellow River, first, Japan must borrow 60 warships to occupy Tanggu and Tianjin, 20 warships to occupy Qingdao, and 20 warships to garrison up and down the Yangtze River. The north and south of the Yellow River can be determined by issuing a proclamation. Second, borrow 100 airplanes to disrupt the military morale in the rear of Tianjin and Jehol. Third, the warships and airplanes should all fly the flag of the Sino-Federal Empire. (4) The Japanese and Manchu governments should secretly prepare a military expenditure of 10 million yuan for Shandong within a possible scope, 5 million yuan for Shanxi, 5 million yuan for Hebei, 20 million yuan for the provinces along the Yangtze River, 20 million yuan for Guangdong and Guangxi, and 20 million yuan for the temporary scale of construction of the new country, which will be allocated from the counter-property of Manchuria. (5) Japan and Manchuria should first send secret envoys to detail the permanent basic treaty of the Sino-Federal Empire, and neither party shall disclose it. (6) Before the military occupation of Tianjin and Peking, the Manchu executive should announce the constitution and prepare the plan for the restoration of power and the facilities of the imperial family with the consent of Japan. (7) After the Sino-Japanese secret treaty is signed, the Manchu executive should telegraph the whole country and secretly send representatives to prepare for the restoration ceremony. (8) After the Sino-Federal Empire occupies Tianjin and Peking, the ambassadors of various countries stationed in Peking and the ambassadors of various countries who once signed the treaty protecting the Qing Empire will discuss and send ambassadors to each other, and discuss the plan of the Sino-Federal Empire to eliminate communism and resist Soviet aggression. (9) After the Sino-Federal Empire occupies Tianjin and Peking, it will convene a federal conference to deliberate on the Sino-Federal Constitution and exchange strategies for the construction of China. (10) Because of the friendship of Japan's help to the Sino-Federal Empire, the Sino-Federal Empire will sincerely organize the Sino-Japanese Economic League, the Industrial League, and various committees to plan the grand plan of various economic industries of the Sino-Federal Empire. Military affairs will be determined separately. (11) Manchuria and Guangdong or other provinces with special circumstances may be allowed by the constitution to use special organizations for independent help. The provinces in the central and northern Yellow River are divided into two systems: one is an autonomous state, and the other is a mandated state. (12) The heads of various religions of the Sino-Federal Empire should be concurrently led by the emperor, but the people are allowed to believe freely. (13) In order to revitalize the industry and roads, the Sino-Federal Empire is allowed to invest in various countries to reside in the interior and abolish concessions.

Wu Suzhou, also known as Wu Yu, from Xuzhou, who used to be a reporter for a certain newspaper, was arrested by the detectives of the Songhu Garrison Command in the autumn of 1930 in cooperation with the police of the Public Concession, and was sent to the First Special District Local Court for adjudication. He was then transferred to the Garrison Command for interrogation. Mr. A reported to Supervisor Lu, pointing out that Wu was still working for the Communist Party, serving as an important position in the Central Committee of the Communist Party, and using the name of a newspaper reporter to secretly inquire about the news of the handling of the Communist Party by various agencies, so as to inform his comrades so that they could escape in advance. So Lu called in Chinese police officer No. 1083 and arrested Wu at the Lao Zha Police Station. The lawyer of the police station, Gan Jingxian, declared that he did not object. Judge Yu then ruled that the officers of the Public Security Bureau should take him away and return him to the case for interrogation.

Solved: Eight Drown in 251

Yushun Ship Collision Case

Compensation of Six Thousand Yuan. The Yushun Wheel of the China Merchants Bureau recently collided with and sank a Jinshunxing fishing boat in the Putuo Sea, killing eight boatmen, including Liu Anbang and Liu Ashi, on the spot. After the accident, the Yushun Wheel rescued 15 people, including Liu Xili. Later, the shipowner Ke Mingshan reported to Yuhuan County that 27 people were on board the ship. In addition to the four people, including Jiang Chunshui, who were rescued by the Liangrixing fishing boat, and the 15 people who were brought to Shanghai by Yushun, eight people drowned in the Bintuo Sea. This matter was of great importance. The Ministry also instructed the bureau to thoroughly investigate the truth and handle it properly. Liu Hongsheng appointed a special commissioner, Zhang Yiming, to conduct an on-site investigation at the scene of the accident to determine the number of casualties. According to the shipowner of Yushun, all the people who fell into the water were rescued and no one died. Zhang Yiming thoroughly investigated the results and confirmed that the number of people who drowned at that time was not as many as eight. According to the loss report submitted by Ke Mingshan, the amount of loss reached more than 10,000 yuan. After many negotiations and several face-to-face talks with the shipowner, the bureau specially expressed sympathy for the fishing boat and paid 6,000 yuan to settle the case. This compensation will be notified by the bureau to the company that underwrote the Yushun Wheel's water insurance, and the company will pay half of the amount. The long-standing collision tragedy has come to an end.

Candidates for the Next Term of Directors

The nine foreign directors of the Shanghai Municipal Council will be elected by taxpayers (foreigners) on March 27th and 28th of this year. According to regulations, anyone with the right to be elected who wishes to stand for election must be nominated in writing by two taxpayers seven days before the election date. The deadline for nominations for this term was noon today (the 18th). The names of those who have been nominated are listed below: Mr. Arnold, Mr. Bell, Mr. Brown, Mr. Franklin, Mr. Funatsu, Mr. Harris, Mr. Lamb, Mr. Latonner, Mr. Lacnodon, Mr. Massey, Mr. Matthey, Mr. Okamoto, Mr. Raven.

In addition, Mr. J.T.W. Brooke has been nominated by two taxpayers to serve as a foreign property commissioner. According to Article 6, Section A of the Property Regulations, he will be considered elected as this year's commissioner.

Idle Talk

Another Iron Proof That China Will Not Perish 262

— Me

A few days ago there was (the pseudo-emperor's relatives) being patriotic, and recently there is the (Guangzhou) famous socialite Ms. Chen, using her charms to save the country.

This is not a problem. When the country is in dire straits, and its demise is imminent, as long as one is a citizen of China, everyone has the responsibility to save the country. (The pseudo-emperor's relatives) are no exception, so (socialites) saving the country is also within reason. Moreover, (a weak woman cannot serve on the battlefield), so of course, she must (use her beauty to serve the country). From this, we can see that there is more than one way to save the country, and (beauty) (charm) can also have a great effect.

However, here we have a very valuable discovery. How many young and handsome young masters, although they may not necessarily regard the country as something external to themselves while chasing after pleasure in singing and dancing halls, cannot but desperately rush to the great love arena. Even spending a thousand gold coins for a smile is worthwhile, let alone just a ten-yuan donation to have (some hope) of keeping a beauty in a golden house. Moreover, they gain the favor of the beauty and also achieve the effect of saving the country. Therefore, they are all worthy people. If China does not perish, of course, they will all have made a great contribution. At the same time, we can more clearly understand that in order to strive for a bright future for the Chinese nation, it is absolutely not necessary for the vast working masses to bear a heavy responsibility, because there are many big figures kowtowing and bowing before the (god of war) who (upholds justice) and (guarantees peace), and there is also this group of young masters who are striving to save the country and are willing to fall at the feet of women, entrusting their patriotism to the goddess of love. If China still must perish, it would truly be too unreasonable.

As for Miss Chen Ruihua, the socialite, loving her country through love letters and charm, it adds even greater glory to our nation. For example, during the First World War, Germany had some female spies who did not hesitate to use their charm to gather enemy intelligence. Even when the Eight-Nation Alliance attacked Beijing, our country also had an unofficial history of prostitutes saving the country. Therefore, beauties saving the country is something that has happened throughout history. There is no need to imitate Mulan and fight on the borderlands amidst the lamentations of Hu Jia and warhorses. Even in the midst of overflowing love and the intoxicating aroma of champagne, one can fulfill a woman's duty to save the country. Compared to the heroines who embroider poems on the tunics of soldiers, how can they be compared?

Since this is the case, such beautiful women and beautiful deeds are of course worthy of being recorded in history to be immortalized. However, before the history of this national crisis has even begun to be compiled, we record it in writing, which is of course also a great merit. Moreover, this is an iron proof that China will not perish. From now on, patriotic people who are worried about the country and the times can rest easy.

Random Notes on Fundraising 263

— Pengnian

Since the news of the fall of Chengde reached our school, the atmosphere of anti-Japanese national salvation in our school has suddenly become tense again. The self-proclaimed patriotic general Chen is running around and shouting, extremely busy. The dancing doctorate Dong has not been to the amusement palace for several days, as if realizing that dancing alone cannot save the country. The political figure Mr. B is also spouting his wonderful theories of national salvation. The student union and the comrade association are all working hard to carry out anti-Japanese work. Judging from the situation, there is no one in our school who is not doing the work of resisting Japan and saving the country.

Yesterday morning, Chen invited me to join their fundraising team. Of course, I couldn't refuse. After breakfast, I followed them to Avenue Joffre, soliciting donations from house to house along the way. At the intersection of Rue Amiral Courbet, a pair of Western-dressed animals came towards us, holding the hand of a fashionable lady with a peachy face and apricot lips. When we saw them, we were extremely welcome! We issued an emergency mobilization order, surrounded them heavily, and stretched out our hands like beggars to ask for money. Alas! Originally, in our ideal, we thought we could certainly win their sympathy and get them to donate some money, but the reality often exceeded expectations. Not only did they not give a single penny, but one of them, wearing full silk-rimmed glasses, scolded us and said: (Shameless things, asking us for money, slow down! slow down!) When we heard this, we were really angry. What do they take us for? How hateful and deplorable!

After lunch, we headed towards Nanking Road. At the intersection of Route Maetthaeur, the Lu family made us angry again. Logically, (when we entered the door, we should first say a few flattering words, and then talk about how loyal and brave the volunteer army is in killing the enemy! How saving the country is saving oneself! How donating military funds is better than chanting Buddha and burning incense, and so on. After shouting all this, then shout a few times to the old man and old woman, asking them to generously donate and participate in this good cause.) After we said the above paragraph once, twice, but they looked at us as if we were something, not saying a word or answering. After we shouted more than ten times (old man and old woman), they finally showed their mature air and said to us:

(You students are really not good at yourselves, unwilling to study hard, and like to do this kind of thing.) (Now that you are here, take two dimes.) After saying this, they took out two small silver coins from their pocket and gave them to us. We had no choice but to leave resentfully under their contemptuous gaze.

Stalking 264

— Hong

Slowly walk, slowly walk!

Where do you live? Tell me;

Oh, looking at you, you are quite pretty. You are probably getting along in years this year, very good;

Hey, what's the reason; are you walking faster? Open socialising, having friends is also good!

Let's go open a room.

The time is dusk. From the moment the grey-blue is about to emerge from the east, groups of female workers on the road are all squeezing towards that huge and solemn factory. Yes, driven by hunger and dominated by the environment! Some are walking slowly through the dense fog on wheelbarrows, and some are far away from the factory; even riding wheelbarrows is impossible, so the extent of their suffering can be imagined. The workers, who live like cattle and horses, have now finished their twelve hours of work and are leaving work! She, walking towards her destination home, yawned a few long yawns, obviously her spirit was extremely exhausted, but when she goes home from work every day, someone is always entangled with her, a white-faced little fat man is stalking her, hoping to eat a piece of her flesh! Naturally, today will be no exception, he is behind her, sometimes to the left, sometimes to the right, sometimes fast, sometimes slow, chasing after her with a smiling face.

Because her home is far away from the factory, every time the little fat man stalks her for a hundred or two hundred steps, the result is only enjoying her cold and sharp glares.

Page 23

The factory whistle blares, and from this sound a group of extremely tired female workers emerge. So the white-faced little fat man is about to start doing his daily homework 丨丨 stalking.

(Hey, girl. It's awfully cold today. Is sleeping alone cold? Okay, let's go open a room to play.)

(Old man, do you know who I am? Get lost!) Her husband, who had been avoiding her from afar, walked up to the little fat man and said. This was just to warn him that she was a married woman, and that a toad should not think of eating swan meat.

(Damn it. Okay, I recognise you, what are you going to do?) At this time, the little fat man became angry and asked back fiercely.

(How unreasonable, you dare to flirt with my woman?)

(Your woman? Heh!)

(You Don't believe it? Do you really want to stalk) me? Bastard!

(Bullshit!)

(Hmm!)

(Hit him, everyone come, hit this pig.)

(I'm hurt, I'm hurt!) she shouted. Suddenly, several fellow men rushed from the west and together they punched and kicked her husband violently. Although he struggled desperately to the death, he could not defeat them. In a moment, he lost consciousness and could not move, falling to the ground! She cried out in shock, (Thank you! Oh no, it's really going to turn into murder, stop it! Stop it.)

He is hurt, he is really hurt; from now on, where will she have the courage to go to work? Alas, (stalking) is so harmful!

Thief 266

— Ping

Near dusk, a gust of wind blew up, and the small road in front of the door leading to the market town was full of flying dust. The children of the neighbors were calling out to their livestock. In this small village, raising livestock is their only occupation, and every family has hundreds or ten chickens and ducks, which is a common thing. Their parents for food and clothing all year round are on the livestock, so their guarding against livestock is the first big thing. If they find traces of a weasel nearby, they are even more on guard day and night.

Zhenmin was sitting on the stone steps in front of the door, thinking about what happened last year

On a snowy day, Dad, Mom, and himself searched all over for a chicken that had been lost at dusk, and later found the chicken drowned in the water by the riverbank. Dad picked up its stiff legs and smiled and said: (A good feast.)

Li Zhenmin's family is the wealthiest in the village, and their life is of course a little more comfortable than ordinary families. His dad likes to drink a little wine, and every night, the three of them eat around a table. The old man, holding his wine glass, chats about the wild stories he heard from the small tea houses in the market town. His wife and son often listen in a trance. So the old man playfully said: (Don't talk tomorrow, I'll kill a chicken to go with the wine). As a rule, in this village, eating chickens and ducks is not a rare thing, but Li Zhenmin's mother is a person who likes to be vegetarian and recite Buddha. She said: (Our family depends on them to make a living, and we still have to kill them for ourselves to eat, Amitabha! The old man twirled his beard and said: (Selling them to others is also one head per knife.) (That is the sin that others bear!) This is the old lady's reason for reciting the Buddha. So the old man said helplessly, (Cook two chicken eggs, I'll do good deeds to avoid one head per knife in the future.) Li Zhenmin couldn't help but laugh at this time. But the old lady still said solemnly: (Doing good deeds will have good rewards!) So when the old man found the drowned chicken, he smiled and said: (A good feast:)

Li Zhenmin was sitting on the stone steps in front of the door, thinking about what happened last year:

Three days after eating the chicken, Dad caught a cold from the wine and was bedridden, feverish, and delirious. Mom joked and said: (You're greedy for chicken, and the old man in the sky is punishing you with two days of illness.) People in the countryside originally regarded fever and cold as common occurrences, and they would get better by eating a little ginger and brown sugar soup. However, Dad's illness did not improve, but worsened every day. Mom became anxious and went to the market to invite a famous doctor. The doctor said that the cold had entered the spleen and stomach, and the prescriptions he prescribed were all very expensive. Dad was ill for three months, and Mom was so thin that she was out of shape. All the chickens and ducks were sold at a low price because they needed money in the cold weather, but Dad finally died of his illness.

He saw the children of the neighbors calling out to their livestock in the dust, and he couldn't help but shed tears. His mom called him from the house to come in and eat. He wiped his tears and saw two bowls of porridge on the table. Mom asked him why his eyes were red. He said that sand had blown into them. The mother and son ate the meal in a haphazard manner and went to bed. Zhenmin thought to himself that there was still porridge to drink today, but what would they eat tomorrow? Hearing Mom tossing and turning in bed, he decided on an idea, staring at the top of the mosquito net waiting for Mom's snoring.

Suddenly, the dogs in the nearby village barked madly, and the old lady woke up from her sleep. There was already the sound of banging on the door, shouting for her son, but there was no answer. He vaguely heard outside the door: (Old woman, come out, your son has done something

Shop Employees' Communication

Marrying a Cousin 267

Editor Sir:

I have a difficult matter, and I would be grateful if you could take the trouble to answer it. The fact is this: I was eleven years old when my father passed away; thanks to my uncle's upbringing, I studied with my cousin. I have two female cousins, and my second cousin has a very good feeling for me. When I lived in her house, she took good care of me. All my clothes were washed and made by her: and when I had free time, we would talk and laugh, which was very happy. Time passed quickly, and in a blink of an eye I was seventeen years old, so I entrusted a relative or friend to recommend me to a yarn shop in this port to learn a trade: it has been five years since then. In these five years, I have often gone to her house, and we are not too estranged. Last September, my aunt suggested to me that she was willing to betroth my second cousin to me, and told me to work hard at my studies and save money to prepare for our marriage in the future. At that time, because I was still young, and I didn't know what my cousin's intentions were, I didn't agree immediately. Another reason was that I knew myself that I was a person without permanent property, and I didn't have much ability to serve society, so I couldn't get a reward to support my family. Even if I got married, I wouldn't have any happiness, and I would be harming my second cousin. Now I have an opportunity to find out what my cousin's intentions are: she said that she is willing to marry me; and she said that her father is a little unwilling, but with her and her mother's intentions, her uncle has no way to stop it. Three years ago, there was an American student studying abroad, who was the son of my uncle's friend, and my uncle had a great interest in marrying my second cousin to him, but my cousin was unwilling. She said that she would rather suffer with me than enjoy happiness with him. This is what she just told me now, expressing her heart. Sir, I am already twenty-one years old now, but I am still a small employee in a store, with a monthly salary of five yuan; in the near future, it will be very difficult to organize a family. But she keeps saying that she is willing to marry me. I have told her that I cannot marry you until my economic ability is sufficient to organize a family. She said that she is willing to wait for me. I advised her to find another suitable husband, and she said (I would rather die, and it is impossible to marry another person). Sir, I have now told you all the facts, and I hope you can answer the following questions for me.

(1) What kind of method can I use to persuade her to marry someone else?

(2) If she insists on not agreeing, how should I treat her? Because in the near future, I will not have the ability to support a family, and I do not want her to waste her precious youth.

(3) She and I have a blood relationship. Although there is no explicit provision in the law prohibiting marriage between cousins, I think that the children born in the future will be affected by the relationship between the parents' bloodline, and there will be some physiological impact. I wonder if you think so?

I hope that you will answer the above three questions in detail. I am very much looking forward to it. I wish you

Peace Shen Shichang bowed

Editor's Note: Zhao Jun's cousin, because she grew up with Zhao Jun since she was a child, she certainly has an accurate understanding of everything about Zhao Jun. Judging from the fact that she is willing to marry him, Zhao Jun must have some outstanding qualities; that is why she is willing to endure some hardships now. We can see this lady's eyesight from the fact that she does not admire vanity and is unwilling to marry a foreign student. We see that more than half of the foreign students have been abroad, so their vision is naturally very high. At the very least, unless you are a college student, you are qualified to be his wife. Zhao Jun's uncle is still thinking about it, which is really pitiful. Therefore, although Zhao Jun's uncle may have some objections, it is not a problem. Moreover, judging from the letter, your aunt and cousin seem to be able to control your uncle! As for the current income, it is not enough to organize a family: fortunately, your cousin is willing to wait. The ancients said (a man marries at thirty), Zhao Jun is now twenty-one years old, and it is not too late to wait another nine years; in these nine years, with his own efforts, success is not difficult.
